MAGMA IMPLICATION ORACLE
Task: Does equation E1 imply equation E2 over all magmas (sets with binary op *)?

ALGORITHM:
1. Check RULES (fast structural tests)
2. Normalize E1,E2: remove all spaces
3. Find E1 in [MAP] to get its class C_a
4. Find E2 in [MAP] to get its class C_b
5. If C_a = C_b -> TRUE
6. Check [EDGES]: if path from C_a to C_b -> TRUE, else FALSE
NOTE: If equation not found in MAP, it is singleton-forcing (implies everything) -> TRUE

[RULES]
R1 SINGLETON: If E1 has a bare variable on one side COMPLETELY ABSENT from the other side -> answer TRUE.
   Test: Look at each side. If one side is just a single letter (x,y,z,w,u) AND that letter does NOT appear ANYWHERE on the other side -> TRUE.
   YES: 'x = y * z' (x not on RHS). 'x = y * (z * w)'. 'x = (y * z) * w'. 'x = y * (y * z)' (x not on RHS).
   NO: 'x = x * y' (x on both sides). 'x = y * (x * z)' (x on both sides).
R2 IDENTITY: If E2 is 'x = x' -> TRUE (everything implies trivial identity).
R3 ABSORPTION LEFT: If E1 = 'x = x * EXPR' where EXPR has var(s) other than x -> E1's class implies x=x*y (class C4).
   Then if E2 = 'x = x * ANYTHING' -> TRUE.
R4 ABSORPTION RIGHT: If E1 = 'x = EXPR * x' where EXPR has var(s) other than x -> E1's class implies x=y*x (class C5).
   Then if E2 = 'x = ANYTHING * x' -> TRUE.
R5 BALANCE: Count * operators on LHS and RHS separately.
   If E1 has SAME count on both sides (balanced) but E2 has DIFFERENT counts (unbalanced),
   and E1 is NOT singleton-forcing -> FALSE.
R6 COUNTEREXAMPLE MAGMAS (any one satisfies E1 but violates E2 -> FALSE):
   LEFT_PROJ {0,1} a*b=a: Satisfies eq iff leftmost variable is same on both sides
   RIGHT_PROJ {0,1} a*b=b: Satisfies eq iff rightmost variable is same on both sides
   CONSTANT {0,1} a*b=0: Satisfies eq iff both sides have at least one *
R7 If E2 = 'x = y' (forces singleton) and E1 is NOT singleton-forcing -> FALSE.

[MAP]
Format: C<class_id>: eq1 | eq2 | ...
Equations NOT listed here are singleton-forcing (use R1: answer TRUE for any E2).
To find an equation: remove spaces from the given equation text, search below.
C1: x=x
C3: x=x*x
C4: x=x*y | x=x*(y*z) | x=x*(y*(x*z)) | x=x*(y*(y*z)) | x=x*(y*(z*y)) | x=x*(y*(z*z)) | x=x*(y*(z*w)) | x=x*((y*z)*z) | x=x*((y*z)*w) | x=x*(y*(x*(y*z))) | x=x*(y*(x*(z*w))) | x=x*(y*(y*(x*z))) | x=x*(y*(y*(y*z))) | x=x*(y*(y*(z*w))) | x=x*(y*(z*(x*y))) | x=x*(y*(z*(x*z))) | x=x*(y*(z*(x*w))) | x=x*(y*(z*(y*y))) | x=x*(y*(z*(y*w))) | x=x*(y*(z*(z*z))) | x=x*(y*(z*(z*w))) | x=x*(y*(z*(w*y))) | x=x*(y*(z*(w*z))) | x=x*(y*(z*(w*w))) | x=x*(y*(z*(w*u))) | x=x*(y*((x*x)*z)) | x=x*(y*((x*y)*z)) | x=x*(y*((x*z)*y)) | x=x*(y*((x*z)*z)) | x=x*(y*((x*z)*w)) | x=x*(y*((y*x)*z)) | x=x*(y*((y*y)*z)) | x=x*(y*((y*z)*w)) | x=x*(y*((z*x)*y)) | x=x*(y*((z*x)*z)) | x=x*(y*((z*x)*w)) | x=x*(y*((z*y)*y)) | x=x*(y*((z*y)*w)) | x=x*(y*((z*z)*z)) | x=x*(y*((z*z)*w)) | x=x*(y*((z*w)*y)) | x=x*(y*((z*w)*z)) | x=x*(y*((z*w)*w)) | x=x*(y*((z*w)*u)) | x=x*((y*z)*(x*y)) | x=x*((y*z)*(x*w)) | x=x*((y*z)*(y*y)) | x=x*((y*z)*(y*w)) | x=x*((y*z)*(z*z)) | x=x*((y*z)*(z*w)) | x=x*((y*z)*(w*y)) | x=x*((y*z)*(w*z)) | x=x*((y*z)*(w*w)) | x=x*((y*z)*(w*u)) | x=x*((y*(x*y))*z) | x=x*((y*(x*z))*w) | x=x*((y*(y*x))*z) | x=x*((y*(y*z))*w) | x=x*((y*(z*x))*z) | x=x*((y*(z*x))*w) | x=x*((y*(z*y))*w) | x=x*((y*(z*z))*z) | x=x*((y*(z*z))*w) | x=x*((y*(z*w))*z) | x=x*((y*(z*w))*w) | x=x*((y*(z*w))*u) | x=x*(((y*z)*z)*z) | x=x*(((y*z)*z)*w) | x=x*(((y*z)*w)*z) | x=x*(((y*z)*w)*w) | x=x*(((y*z)*w)*u)
